LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [k0].[UserId], [k0].[RoleId], [k0].[Discriminator], [k0].[KorisniciId], [k0].[UlogeId], [u].[Id], [u].[ConcurrencyStamp], [u].[Name], [u].[NormalizedName]

ORDER BY [k].[Id], [t].[UserId], [t].[RoleId]
